</tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         September 10\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 September 16\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         150\xc2\xa0km/h (90\xc2\xa0mph)\n         <small>\n          (10-min)\n         </small>\n         955\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Typhoon_Doksuri_(2017)" title="Typhoon Doksuri (2017)">\n        Typhoon Doksuri (2017)\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       As of September 19, the NDRRMC confirmed a total of 8 dead due to landslides and flooding while total damages were up to Ph\xe2\x82\xb1267 million (US$5.23 million).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Doksuri1_117-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Doksuri1-117">\n         [116]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       On September 15, Typhoon Doksuri made landfall in Qu\xe1\xba\xa3ng B\xc3\xacnh Province, Vietnam as a Category 3 typhoon. Doksuri killed 15 people so far in Vietnam while estimated damages were about \xe2\x82\xab16.36 trillion (US$720 million).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Doksuri2_118-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Doksuri2-118">\n         [117]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Doksuri3_119-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Doksuri3-119">\n         [118]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Doksuri5_120-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Doksuri5-120">\n         [119]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Despite making landfall in Indochina, Doksuri affected Hainan and total economic losses were estimated to be CNY 59 million(USD 8.96 million).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Doksuri4_121-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Doksuri4-121">\n         [120]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="Tropical_Depression_22W_(Nando)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Depression_22W_.28Nando.29">\n        Tropical Depression 22W (Nando)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Tropical Depression 22W (Nando)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #5ebaff">\n         Tropical depression\xc2\xa0(JMA)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #5ebaff">\n         Tropical depression\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Nando_2017-09-25_0335Z.jpg">\n            <img alt="Nando 2017-09-25 0335Z.jpg" data-file-height="8017" data-file-width="5793" //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7e/Nando_2017-09-25_0335Z.jpg/300px-Nando_2017-09-25_0335Z.jpg 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Nando_2017_track.png">\n            <img alt="Nando 2017 track.png" data-file-height="1669" data-file-width="2700" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7a/Nando_2017_track.png/150px-Nando_2017_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7a/Nando_2017_track.png/225px-Nando_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7a/Nando_2017_track.png/300px-Nando_2017_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         September 23\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 September 25\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         55\xc2\xa0km/h (35\xc2\xa0mph)\n         <small>\n          (10-min)\n         </small>\n         1002\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       A tropical depression formed to the west of Luzon on September 23, and was named "Nando" by PAGASA. The tropical depression quickly moved west-northwest and made landfall in Qu\xe1\xba\xa3ng Ninh, Vietnam, on September 25, before dissipating later on the same day.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The China Observatory issued a "yellow" alert over in the eastern and southern regions due to rainstorms. Some areas have warned a possible precipitation of about 140\xc2\xa0mm (5.5\xc2\xa0in).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-122">\n        <a href="#cite_note-122">\n         [121]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Typhoon Signal No. 1 was raised over in\n       <a href="/wiki/Hong_Kong" title="Hong Kong">\n        Hong Kong\n       </a>\n       during September 24, with expected gusts of up to 70\xc2\xa0km/h (42\xc2\xa0mph) including rough swells.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-123">\n        <a href="#cite_note-123">\n         [122]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       A voltage dip also occurred, causing 17 people to be trapped in lifts.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-124">\n        <a href="#cite_note-124">\n         [123]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       As the depression approached\n       <a href="/wiki/Vietnam" title="Vietnam">\n        Vietnam\n       </a>\n       on September 25, the Vietnam National Center for Hydro-Meteorological Forecasting of Vietnam forecast rainfall of about 150\xc2\xa0mm (5.9\xc2\xa0in) in\n       <a href="/wiki/Hanoi" title="Hanoi">\n        Hanoi\n       </a>\n       and surrounding provinces, with rough waves up to 3\xc2\xa0m (9.8\xc2\xa0ft) in\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ha_Long_Bay" title="Ha Long Bay">\n        Ha Long Bay\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-125">\n        <a href="#cite_note-125">\n         [124]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Depression_23W">\n        Tropical Depression 23W\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Tropical Depression 23W">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #5ebaff">\n         Tropical depression\xc2\xa0(JMA)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #5ebaff">\n         Tropical depression\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:23W_2017-10-08_0610Z.jpg">\n            <img alt="23W 2017-10-08 0610Z.jpg" data-file-height="3501" data-file-width="2416" height="217" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/31/23W_2017-10-08_0610Z.jpg/150px-23W_2017-10-08_0610Z.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/31/23W_2017-10-08_0610Z.jpg/225px-23W_2017-10-08_0610Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/31/23W_2017-10-08_0610Z.jpg/300px-23W_2017-10-08_0610Z.jpg 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:23W_2017_track.png">\n            <img alt="23W 2017 track.png" data-file-height="1669" data-file-width="2700" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/23W_2017_track.png/150px-23W_2017_track.png" //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/23W_2017_track.png/300px-23W_2017_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         October 7\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 October 10\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         55\xc2\xa0km/h (35\xc2\xa0mph)\n         <small>\n          (10-min)\n         </small>\n         1000\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_Depression_23W" title="Tropical Depression 23W">\n        Tropical Depression 23W\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Early on October 7, a tropical depression formed to the west of the Philippines.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-126">\n        <a href="#cite_note-126">\n         [125]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Early on October 10, the tropical depression made landfall in H\xc3\xa0 T\xc4\xa9nh Province, Vietnam, and dissipated shortly afterward. Consequently, both the JMA and the JTWC issued their final advisories for the storm.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Tropical Depression 23W caused severe flooding over provinces of Northern and Central Vietnam. Roughly more than 700 houses have been destroyed, while rescue efforts have saved 28 people from the danger zone. So far at least 83 people were killed, and damages were about 9.27 trillion\xe2\x82\xab (US$409 million).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-23W1_127-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-23W1-127">\n         [126]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-23W2_128-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-23W2-128">\n         [127]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       During October 10, the\n       <a href="/wiki/Red_River_(Asia)" title="Red River (Asia)">\n        Red River\n       </a>\n       was forecast to have waters exceed to the levels of 3\xe2\x80\x9350\xc2\xa0cm (2\xe2\x80\x9320\xc2\xa0in).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-129">\n        <a href="#cite_note-129">\n         [128]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-130">\n        <a href="#cite_note-130">\n         [129]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In Ho\xc3\xa0ng Long river (Ninh B\xc3\xacnh Province) flooding was the most severe since 1985.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-131">\n        <a href="#cite_note-131">\n         [130]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="Typhoon_Khanun_(Odette)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Typhoon_Khanun_.28Odette.29">\n        Typhoon Khanun (Odette)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Typhoon Khanun (Odette)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #fdaf9a">\n         Typhoon\xc2\xa0(JMA)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ffe775">\n         Category 2\xc2\xa0typhoon\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Khanun_2017-10-15_0310Z.jpg">\n            <img </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         October 11\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 October 16\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         150\xc2\xa0km/h (90\xc2\xa0mph)\n         <small>\n          (10-min)\n         </small>\n         950\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <table class="plainlinks metadata ambox mbox-small-left ambox-content" role="presentation">\n       <tr>\n        <td class="mbox-image">\n         <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg">\n          <img alt="[icon]" data-file-height="31" data-file-width="44" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/20px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/30px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/40px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png 2x" width="20"/>\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td class="mbox-text">\n         <div class="mbox-text-span">\n          <b>\n           This section needs expansion\n          </b>\n          .\n          <small>\n           You can help by\n           <a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=">\n            adding to it\n           </a>\n           .\n          </small>\n          <small>\n           <i>\n            (October 2017)\n           </i>\n          </small>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       According to the NDRRMC, Khanun killed only one person, with total damages of Php4.45 million (US$86,400).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Khanun4_132-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Khanun4-132">\n         [131]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Total economic damages in Mainland China amounted to CNY 1.35 billion (USD 203.8 million), including 430 million CNY in Zhejiang province, 848 million CNY in Guangdong Province, 70 million in Hainan.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Khanun1_133-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Khanun1-133">\n         [132]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Khanun2_134-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Khanun2-134">\n         [133]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Khanun3_135-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Khanun3-135">\n         [134]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Authorities in Hong Kong and Macau raised the number 8 tropical cyclone warning on October 15 as gale-force winds affected the region.\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="Typhoon_Lan_(Paolo)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Typhoon_Lan_.28Paolo.29">\n        Typhoon Lan (Paolo)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Typhoon Lan (Paolo)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #fdaf9a">\n         Typhoon\xc2\xa0(JMA)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ff8f20">\n         Category 4\xc2\xa0super\xc2\xa0typhoon\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Lan_2017-10-21_0412Z.jpg">\n            <img alt="Lan 2017-10-21 0412Z.jpg" data-file-height="4800" data-file-width="3600" height="200" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2c/Lan_2017-10-21_0412Z.jpg/150px-Lan_2017-10-21_0412Z.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2c/Lan_2017-10-21_0412Z.jpg/225px-Lan_2017-10-21_0412Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2c/Lan_2017-10-21_0412Z.jpg/300px-Lan_2017-10-21_0412Z.jpg 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Lan_2017_track.png">\n            <img alt="Lan 2017 track.png" data-file-height="2700" data-file-width="2700" height="150"    <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         October 14\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 October 23\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         175\xc2\xa0km/h (110\xc2\xa0mph)\n         <small>\n          (10-min)\n         </small>\n         925\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Typhoon_Lan" title="Typhoon Lan">\n        Typhoon Lan\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States_Naval_Research_Laboratory" title="United States Naval Research Laboratory">\n        United States Naval Research Laboratory\n       </a>\n       (NRL) initially mentioned a tropical disturbance over\n       <a href="/wiki/Chuuk_State" title="Chuuk State">\n        Chuuk\n       </a>\n       on October 11.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-136">\n        <a href="#cite_note-136">\n         [135]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       After the slow consolidation, the\n       <a href="/wiki/Joint_Typhoon_Warning_Center" title="Joint Typhoon Warning Center">\n        Joint Typhoon Warning Center\n       </a>\n       (JTWC) issued a\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_Cyclone_Formation_Alert" title="Tropical Cyclone Formation Alert">\n        Tropical Cyclone Formation Alert\n       </a>\n       to the elongated system early on October 14,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-137">\n        <a href="#cite_note-137">\n         [136]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       shortly after the\n       <a href="/wiki/Japan_Meteorological_Agency" title="Japan Meteorological Agency">\n        Japan Meteorological Agency\n       </a>\n       (JMA) started to monitor it as a\n       <a href="/wiki/Low-pressure_area" title="Low-pressure area">\n        low-pressure area\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-138">\n        <a href="#cite_note-138">\n         [137]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The agency upgraded it to a tropical depression almost one day later and began to issue tropical cyclone warnings since 06:00\n       <a href="/wiki/Coordinated_Universal_Time" title="Coordinated Universal Time">\n        UTC\n       </a>\n       on October 15.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-139">\n        <a href="#cite_note-139">\n         [138]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-140">\n        <a href="#cite_note-140">\n         [139]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In the afternoon, the JTWC also upgraded it to a tropical depression assigning the designation\n       <i>\n        25W\n       </i>\n       , which formative but shallow convective\n       <a href="/wiki/Rainband" title="Rainband">\n        bands\n       </a>\n       had become more organized, and symmetrically wrapped into a defined low-level circulation center.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-141">\n        <a href="#cite_note-141">\n         [140]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       About three hours later, the JMA upgraded it to the twenty-first Northwest Pacific tropical storm in 2017 and assigned the international name\n       <i>\n        Lan\n       </i>\n       , when it was located approximately 310\xc2\xa0km (190\xc2\xa0mi) to the northeast of\n       <a href="/wiki/Palau" title="Palau">\n        Palau\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-142">\n        <a href="#cite_note-142">\n         [141]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Early on October 16, the JTWC upgraded Lan to a tropical storm too, based on T-number 2.5 of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Dvorak_technique" title="Dvorak technique">\n        Dvorak technique\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-143">\n        <a href="#cite_note-143">\n         [142]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       shortly before it entered the Philippine Area of Responsibility and received the name\n       <i>\n        Paolo\n       </i>\n       from\n       <a href="/wiki/PAGASA" title="PAGASA">\n        PAGASA\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-144">\n        <a href="#cite_note-144">\n         [143]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Total economic losses from the communal facilities in Mainland Japan were counted to be JPY 13.748 billion (USD 120.53 million).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Lan1_145-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Lan1-145">\n         [144]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Lan2_146-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Lan2-146">\n         [145]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Total economic losses from the agriculture facilities in Mainland Japan were counted to be JPY 10.8 billion (USD 94.68 million).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Lan3_147-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Lan3-147">\n         [146]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Depression_26W">\n        Tropical Depression 26W\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Tropical Depression 26W">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #5ebaff">\n         Tropical depression\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:26W_2017-10-19_0550Z.jpg">\n            <img alt="26W 2017-10-19 0550Z.jpg" data-file-height="6881" data-file-width="5281" height="195" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/26W_2017-10-19_0550Z.jpg/150px-26W_2017-10-19_0550Z.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/26W_2017-10-19_0550Z.jpg/225px-26W_2017-10-19_0550Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/26W_2017-10-19_0550Z.jpg/300px-26W_2017-10-19_0550Z.jpg 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:26W_2017_track.png">\n            <img alt="26W 2017 track.png" data-file-height="1669" data-file-width="2700" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/08/26W_2017_track.png/150px-26W_2017_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/08/26W_2017_track.png/225px-26W_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/08/26W_2017_track.png/300px-26W_2017_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         October 18\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 October 19\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         45\xc2\xa0km/h (30\xc2\xa0mph)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         1002\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       Originating from an enhanced\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Southwest_monsoon" title="Southwest monsoon">\n        monsoon\n       </a>\n       trough, a tropical disturbance developed just to the northwest of\n       <a href="/wiki/Palawan" title="Palawan">\n        Palawan\n       </a>\n       on October 17.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-148">\n        <a href="#cite_note-148">\n         [147]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On October 18, the JTWC had issued a TCFA on the system.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-149">\n        <a href="#cite_note-149">\n         [148]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       By 21:00 UTC of that day, the JTWC began issuing advisories as they classified it as a tropical depression, assigning the identifier\n       <i>\n        26W\n       </i>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-150">\n        <a href="#cite_note-150">\n         [149]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       This was due to deep convection found near the storm\'s center with formative banding, along with its location over in a favorable environment.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-151">\n        <a href="#cite_note-151">\n         [150]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Initially, its forecast stated that 26W would intensify into a weak tropical storm, although due to a disorganized center with strong shear, the JTWC issued their final advisory on October 19 as it was being absorbed by the outflow of nearby\n       <a href="/wiki/Typhoon_Lan" title="Typhoon Lan">\n        Typhoon Lan\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-152">\n        <a href="#cite_note-152">\n         [151]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Associated with the rainbands of a nearby typhoon, 26W helped spread scattered rainfall throughout most of\n       <a href="/wiki/Visayas" title="Visayas">\n        Visayas\n       </a>\n       and northern\n       <a href="/wiki/Mindanao" title="Mindanao">\n        Mindanao\n       </a>\n       . Residents in some areas were alerted against possible flash floods and landslides.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-153">\n        <a href="#cite_note-153">\n         [152]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       14 people were dead from heavy rainfall from the system and its precursor, and raised a\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/State_of_calamity" title="State of calamity">\n        state of calamity\n       </a>\n       in\n       <a href="/wiki/Zamboanga_City" title="Zamboanga City">\n        Zamboanga City\n       </a>\n       on October 23.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-154">\n        <a href="#cite_note-154">\n         [153]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-26W1_155-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-26W1-155">\n         [154]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="Severe_Tropical_Storm_Saola_(Quedan)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Severe_Tropical_Storm_Saola_.28Quedan.29">\n        Severe Tropical Storm Saola (Quedan)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Severe Tropical Storm Saola (Quedan)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ccffff">\n         Severe tropical storm\xc2\xa0(JMA)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ffffcc">\n         Category 1\xc2\xa0typhoon\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Saola_2017-10-28_0250Z.png">\n            <img alt="Saola 2017-10-28 0250Z.png" data-file-height="2280" data-file-width="1710" height="200" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/60/Saola_2017-10-28_0250Z.png/150px-Saola_2017-10-28_0250Z.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/60/Saola_2017-10-28_0250Z.png/225px-Saola_2017-10-28_0250Z.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/60/Saola_2017-10-28_0250Z.png/300px-Saola_2017-10-28_0250Z.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Saola_2017_track.png">\n            <img alt="Saola 2017 track.png" data-file-height="2700" data-file-width="2700" height="150" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3c/Saola_2017_track.png/150px-Saola_2017_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3c/Saola_2017_track.png/225px-Saola_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3c/Saola_2017_track.png/300px-Saola_2017_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         October 19\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 October 29\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         110\xc2\xa0km/h (70\xc2\xa0mph)\n         <small>\n          (10-min)\n         </small>\n         975\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       A tropical depression formed north of Guam, the next day, the Tropical Depression transitioned into a Tropical Storm and the Japan Meteorological Agency named it Tropical Storm Saola. By evening of that day, Saola entered the Philippine Area of Responsibility (PAR). The PAGASA gave the local name "Quedan" to the storm. By the next day, Saola moved slowly and strengthened into a severe tropical storm. Its intensity did not change, even as high wind shear occurred to the north of Saola and the strengthening northeast monsoon while heading to Japan. It started weakening while in cold waters and brought rains to Southern Japan but did not make landfall. It dissipated after avoiding Japan and heading northeast.\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Depression_29W">\n        Tropical Depression 29W\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Tropical Depression 29W">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2"       1006\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       The JMA upgraded a low-pressure area to a tropical depression over the southern portion of the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/South_China_sea" title="South China sea">\n        South China sea\n       </a>\n       on October 30.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-156">\n        <a href="#cite_note-156">\n         [155]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The JTWC issued a TCFA during the next day as it gathered strength. Initially forecast to intensify to a tropical storm, the system rapidly deteriorated and degenerated to a remnant low on November 3 as it tracked into the\n       <a href="/wiki/Gulf_of_Thailand" title="Gulf of Thailand">\n        Gulf of Thailand\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-157">\n        <a href="#cite_note-157">\n         [156]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Over in the course of two days, after re-curving back to the gulf, the JTWC re-issued a TCFA.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-158">\n        <a href="#cite_note-158">\n         [157]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       By November 6, the JTWC classified the system as Tropical Depression 29W.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-159">\n        <a href="#cite_note-159">\n         [158]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       It caused unusually heavy rains and flash floods to occur in the state of\n       <a href="/wiki/Penang" title="Penang">\n        Penang\n       </a>\n       , killing 7 people.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-160">\n        <a href="#cite_note-160">\n         [159]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Flood waters in parts of the city reached 3.7\xc2\xa0m (12\xc2\xa0ft), submerging entire homes.\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="Typhoon_Damrey_(Ramil)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Typhoon_Damrey_.28Ramil.29">\n        Typhoon Damrey (Ramil)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Typhoon Damrey (Ramil)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #fdaf9a">\n         Typhoon\xc2\xa0(JMA)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ffe775">\n         Category 2\xc2\xa0typhoon\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Typhoon_Damrey_(2017)" title="Typhoon Damrey (2017)">\n        Typhoon Damrey (2017)\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The JMA upgraded a\n       <a href="/wiki/Low-pressure_area" title="Low-pressure area">\n        low-pressure area\n       </a>\n       to a tropical depression east of\n       <a href="/wiki/Visayas" title="Visayas">\n        Visayas\n       </a>\n       on October 31. PAGASA gave warnings to the system and named it\n       <i>\n        Ramil\n       </i>\n       . The storm brought rainy weather on the All Saints\'s Day (November 1) to Visayas. The tropical depression made landfall over\n       <a href="/wiki/Busuanga,_Palawan" title="Busuanga, Palawan">\n        Busuanga, Palawan\n       </a>\n       at midnight on November 1. On November 2, Ramil strengthened, and the JTWC and JMA upgraded Ramil to a tropical storm, and gave the system the international name\n       <i>\n        Damrey\n       </i>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-161">\n        <a href="#cite_note-161">\n         [160]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       As of November 8, a total of 112 people were confirmed dead due to the storm.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Express1_162-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Express1-162">\n         [161]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-163">\n        <a href="#cite_note-163">\n         [162]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n    <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a class="longitude">\n            123\xc2\xb042\xe2\x80\xb2E\n           </span>\n          </span>\n         </span>\n         <span class="geo-multi-punct">\n          \xef\xbb\xbf / \xef\xbb\xbf\n         </span>\n         <span class="geo-default">\n          <span class="vcard">\n           <span class="geo-dec" title="Maps, aerial photos, and other data for this location">\n            13.1\xc2\xb0N 123.7\xc2\xb0E\n           </span>\n           <span style="display:none">\n            \xef\xbb\xbf /\n            <span class="geo">\n             13.1; 123.7\n            </span>\n           </span>\n           <span style="display:none">\n            \xef\xbb\xbf (\n            <span class="fn org">\n             Salome\n            </span>\n            )\n           </span>\n          </span>\n         </span>\n        </a>\n       </span>\n       , about 226 nautical miles (419 kilometres; 260 miles) ESE of\n       <a href="/wiki/Manila" title="Manila">\n        Manila\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">\n        Philippines\n       </a>\n       . 10-minute sustained winds are at 25nbsp;knots (45\xc2\xa0km/h; 30\xc2\xa0mph), while 1-minute sustained winds are at 25\xc2\xa0knots (45\xc2\xa0km/h; 30\xc2\xa0mph), with gusts of up to 35\xc2\xa0knots (65\xc2\xa0km/h; 40\xc2\xa0mph). The minimum barometric pressure is at 1006\n       <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n        hPa\n       </a>\n       (29.71\n       <a href="/wiki/Inch_of_mercury" title="Inch of mercury">\n        inHg\n       </a>\n       ), and the system is moving west slowly.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       For latest official information, see:\n      </p>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n Depression 30W (Thirty)\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        The PAGASA\'S\n        <a class="external text" href="https://pubfiles.pagasa.dost.gov.ph/tamss/weather/bulletin.pdf" rel="nofollow">\n         latest public advisory on Tropical Depression Salome\n        </a>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Watches_and_warnings">\n <tr>\n        <td style="background-color:#5ebaff; width:12.6em; text-align:center; vertical-align: middle;" title="Signal #1 - Winds of 30\xe2\x80\x9360\xc2\xa0km/h (20\xe2\x80\x9337\xc2\xa0mph) are (20\xe2\x80\x9337\xc2\xa0mph) are expected to occur within the next 36\xc2\xa0hours.\n         </i>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <ul>\n          <li>\n           <b>\n            <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/CALABARZON" title="CALABARZON">\n             CALABARZON\n            </a>\n           </b>\n           <small>\n            <i>\n             (Region IV)\n            </i>\n           </small>\n           <ul>\n            <li>\n             Southern\n             <a href="/wiki/Quezon" title="Quezon">\n              Quezon\n             </a>\n            </li>\n         </a>\n            </li>\n           </ul>\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           <b>\n            <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Southwestern_Tagalog_Region" title="Southwestern Tagalog Region">\n             Southwestern Tagalog Region\n            </a>\n           </b>\n           <small>\n            <i>\n             (MIMAROPA)\n            </i>\n           </small>\n           <ul>\n            <li>\n             <a href="/wiki/Romblon" title="Romblon">\n              Romblon\n             </a>\n            </li>\n            <li>\n             <a              Oriental Mindoro\n             </a>\n            </li>\n            <li>\n             <a href="/wiki/Occidental_Mindoro" title="Occidental Mindoro">\n              Occidental Mindoro\n             </a>\n            </li>\n           </ul>\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           <b>\n            <a href="/wiki/Bicol_Region" title="Bicol Region">\n             Bicol Region\n            </a>\n           </b>\n           <small>\n            <i>\n             (Region V)\n            </i>\n           </small>\n           <ul>\n            <li>\n             <a href="/wiki/Camarines_Sur" title="Camarines Sur">\n              Camarines Sur\n             </a>\n            </li>\n            <li>\n             <a href="/wiki/Albay" title="Albay">\n              Albay\n             </a>\n            </li>\n            <li>\n             <a href="/wiki/Sorsogon" title="Sorsogon">\n              Sorsogon\n             </a>\n            </li>\n            <li>\n             <a href="/wiki/Masbate" title="Masbate">\n              Masbate\n             </a>\n             including\n             <a href="/wiki/Ticao_Island" title="Ticao Island">\n              Ticao\n             </a>\n             and\n             <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Burias_Island" title="Burias Island">\n              Burias\n             </a>\n             Islands\n            </li>\n           </ul>\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           <b>\n            <a href="/wiki/Eastern_Visayas" title="Eastern Visayas">\n             Eastern Visayas\n            </a>\n           </b>\n           <small>\n            <i>\n             (Region VIII)\n            </i>\n           </small>\n           <ul>\n            <li>\n             <a href="/wiki/Northern_Samar"    <a href="/wiki/Leyte" title="Leyte">\n              Leyte\n             </a>\n             including\n             <a href="/wiki/Biliran" title="Biliran">\n              Biliran\n             </a>\n            </li>\n           </ul>\n          </li>\n         </ul>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Other_systems">\n        Other systems\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: Other systems">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       On March 19, a tropical depression formed close to the northeast of\n       <a href="/wiki/Mindanao" title="Mindanao">\n        Mindanao\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">\n        Philippines\n       </a>\n       , and dissipated over the\n       <a href="/wiki/Sibuyan_Sea" title="Sibuyan Sea">\n        Sibuyan Sea\n       </a>\n       two days later.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-164">\n        <a href="#cite_note-164">\n         [163]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-165">\n        <a href="#cite_note-165">\n         [164]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Early on June 29, the JMA initiated advisories on a newly formed tropical depression located about 138\xc2\xa0km (86\xc2\xa0mi) south of\n       <a href="/wiki/Okinawa_Island" title="Okinawa Island">\n        Okinawa Island\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-166">\n        <a href="#cite_note-166">\n         [165]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The system re-curved and started moving in a northeastward direction until it dissipated to the southwest of\n       <a href="/wiki/Tokyo" title="Tokyo">\n        Tokyo\n       </a>\n       on July 1.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-167">\n        <a href="#cite_note-167">\n         [166]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Early on July 4, the JMA indicated that a tropical depression had formed about 505\xc2\xa0km (314\xc2\xa0mi) south of\n       <a href="/wiki/Okinotorishima" title="Okinotorishima">\n        Okinotorishima\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-168">\n        <a href="#cite_note-168">\n         [167]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       During the next day, the JTWC issued a\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_Cyclone_Formation_Alert" title="Tropical Cyclone Formation Alert">\n        Tropical Cyclone Formation Alert\n       </a>\n       (TCFA) on the system, although it was canceled several hours later.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-169">\n        <a href="#cite_note-169">\n         [168]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       After moving northward, the depression rapidly weakened as it was absorbed by a\n       <a href="/wiki/Stationary_front" title="Stationary front">\n        stationary front\n       </a>\n       on July 7.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-170">\n        <a href="#cite_note-170">\n         [169]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Early on July 13, the JMA reported that a non-tropical low had transitioned into a tropical depression about 72\xc2\xa0km (45\xc2\xa0mi) north-northeast of\n       <a href="/wiki/Iwo_Jima" title="Iwo Jima">\n        Iwo Jima\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-171">\n        <a href="#cite_note-171">\n         [170]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The depression moved in a generally northeasterly direction until weakening to a low-pressure area by 06:00 UTC on July 16.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-172">\n        <a href="#cite_note-172">\n         [171]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       A tropical depression formed about 691\xc2\xa0km (429\xc2\xa0mi) northeast of\n       <a href="/wiki/Wake_Island" title="Wake Island">\n        Wake Island\n       </a>\n       late on July 25, though the JTWC indicated it as a subtropical system with estimated recorded winds of 65\xc2\xa0km/h (40\xc2\xa0mph).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-173">\n        <a href="#cite_note-173">\n         [172]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-174">\n        <a href="#cite_note-174">\n         [173]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       After several days, the system had already transitioned into an extratropical cyclone on July 29, without becoming a tropical storm.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-175">\n        <a href="#cite_note-175">\n         [174]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Early on August 25 the JMA started to track a tropical depression over in the\n       <a href="/wiki/South_China_Sea" title="South China Sea">\n        South China Sea\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-176">\n        <a href="#cite_note-176">\n         [175]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       although it was last monitored during the next day when it was absorbed by the outflow of\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_Storm_Pakhar_(2017)" title="Tropical Storm Pakhar (2017)">\n        Tropical Storm Pakhar\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-177">\n        <a href="#cite_note-177">\n         [176]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On August 28, the JMA started to issue advisories on a tropical depression that had developed about 1,217\xc2\xa0km (756\xc2\xa0mi) east-northeast of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tuguegarao_City" title="Tuguegarao City">\n        Tuguegarao City\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-178">\n        <a href="#cite_note-178">\n         [177]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The JMA predicted that the system would become a tropical storm within the next 24 hours, although because the system did not develop further, the JMA issued their final advisory on 03:00 UTC of August 29 when the system had weakened into a low-pressure area.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-179">\n        <a href="#cite_note-179">\n         [178]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The remnants of the system helped with formation of Tropical Storm Mawar.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-180">\n        <a href="#cite_note-180">\n         [179]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Storm_names">\n        Storm names\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: Storm names">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       See also:\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclone_naming" title="Tropical cyclone naming">\n        Tropical cyclone naming\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/History_of_tropical_cyclone_naming" title="History of tropical cyclone naming">\n        History of tropical cyclone naming\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Within the Northwest Pacific Ocean, both the\n       <a href="/wiki/Japan_Meteorological_Agency" title="Japan Meteorological Agency">\n        Japan Meteorological Agency\n       </a>\n       (JMA) and PAGASA assign names to tropical cyclones that develop in the Western Pacific, which can result in a tropical cyclone having two names.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Padgett_Dec_99_181-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Padgett_Dec_99-181">\n         [180]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The Japan Meteorological Agency\'s RSMC Tokyo\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x94 Typhoon Center assigns international names to tropical cyclones on behalf of the\n       <a href="/wiki/World_Meteorological_Organization" title="World Meteorological Organization">\n        World Meteorological Organization\n       </a>\n       \'s Typhoon Committee, should they be judged to have 10-minute sustained windspeeds of 65\xc2\xa0km/h (40\xc2\xa0mph).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-TC_182-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-TC-182">\n         [181]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       PAGASA assigns names to tropical cyclones which move into or form as a tropical depression in their area of responsibility located between 135\xc2\xb0E\xe2\x80\x93115\xc2\xb0E and between 5\xc2\xb0N\xe2\x80\x9325\xc2\xb0N even if the cyclone has had an international name assigned to it.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Padgett_Dec_99_181-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Padgett_Dec_99-181">\n         [180]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The names of significant tropical cyclones are retired, by both\n       <a href="/wiki/List_of_retired_Philippine_typhoon_names" title="List of retired Philippine typhoon names">\n        PAGASA\n       </a>\n       and the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_retired_Pacific_typhoon_names_(JMA)" title="List of retired Pacific typhoon names (JMA)">\n        Typhoon Committee\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-TC_182-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-TC-182">\n         [181]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Should the list of names for the Philippine region be exhausted then names will be taken from an auxiliary list of which the first ten are published each season. Unused names are marked in\n       <span style="color:#666666">\n        gray\n       </span>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="International_names">\n        International names\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: International names">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/List_of_retired_Pacific_typhoon_names" title="List of retired Pacific typhoon names">\n        List of retired Pacific typhoon names\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       A tropical cyclone is named when it is judged to have 10-minute sustained windspeeds of 65\xc2\xa0km/h (40\xc2\xa0mph).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-183">\n        <a href="#cite_note-183">\n         [182]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The JMA selected the names from a list of 140 names, that had been developed by the 14 members nations and territories of the\n       <a href="/wiki/List_of_retired_Pacific_typhoon_names#Background" title="List of retired Pacific typhoon names">\n        ESCAP/WMO Typhoon Committee\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Retired_typhoons_184-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Retired_typhoons-184">\n         [183]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Retired names, if any, will be announced by the\n       <a href="/wiki/World_Meteorological_Organization" title="World Meteorological Organization">\n        WMO\n       </a>\n       in 2018; though replacement names will be announced in 2019. The next 28\xc2\xa0names on the naming list are listed here along with their international numeric designation, if they are used. During the season the names\n       <i>\n        Hato\n       </i>\n       and\n       <i>\n        Lan\n       </i>\n       were used for the first time, after it replaced the names\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_Storm_Washi" title="Tropical Storm Washi">\n        Washi\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Typhoon_Vicente" title="Typhoon Vicente">\n        Vicente\n       </a>\n       , which was retired after the\n       <a href="/wiki/2011_Pacific_typhoon_season" title="2011 Pacific typhoon season">\n        2011\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/2012_Pacific_typhoon_season" title="2012 Pacific typhoon season">\n        2012 seasons\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <table style="width:100%;">\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         <ul>\n          <li>\n           Muifa (1701)\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           Merbok (1702)\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           Nanmadol (1703)\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           Talas (1704)\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           Noru (1705)\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           Kulap (1706)\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           Roke (1707)\n          </li>\n         </ul>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <ul>\n          <li>\n           Sonca (1708)\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           Nesat (1709)\n (1715)\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           Mawar (1716)\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           Guchol (1717)\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           Talim (1718)\n          </li>\n            </i>\n           </span>\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           <span style="color:#666666">\n            Bolaven\n            <i>\n             (unused)\n            </i>\n           </span>\n          </li>\n         </ul>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Philippines">\n        Philippines\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Pacific_typhoon_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=40" title="Edit section: Philippines">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/List_of_retired_Philippine_typhoon_names" title="List of retired Philippine typhoon names">\n        List of retired Philippine typhoon names\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       This season, PAGASA will use its own naming scheme for cyclones, that will either develop within or move into their self-defined area of responsibility.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-PAGASA_Names_185-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-PAGASA_Names-185">\n         [184]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The names were taken from a list of names, that was last used during\n       <a href="/wiki/2013_Pacific_typhoon_season" title="2013 Pacific typhoon season">\n        2013\n       </a>\n       and are scheduled to be used again during 2021.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-PAGASA_Names_185-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-PAGASA_Names-185">\n         [184]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       All of the names are the same except for Lannie, Salome and Yasmin, which replaced the names\n       <a href="/wiki/Typhoon_Utor" title="Typhoon Utor">\n        Labuyo\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Typhoon_Nari_(2013)" title="Typhoon Nari (2013)">\n        Santi\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Typhoon_Haiyan" title="Typhoon Haiyan">\n        Yolanda\n       </a>\n       after they were retired.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-PAGASA_Names_185-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-PAGASA_Names-185">\n         [184]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The name Lannie and Salome was used for the first time this year.\n      </p>\n      <table style="width:100%;">\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         <ul>\n          <li>\n           Auring\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           Bising\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           Crising\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           Dante (1701)\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           Emong (1703)\n          </li>\n         </ul>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <ul>\n          <li>\n           Fabian (1707)\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           Gorio            </i>\n           </span>\n          </li>\n         </ul>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Season_effects">\n        Season effects\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n       </a>\n           and\n           <a href="/wiki/Macau" title="Macau">\n            Macau\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </li>\n         <li id="cite_note-Indochina-189">\n
